what&#39;s the best Android Weather app?&quot;<br>Brighthub *****<p>WeatherPro for Android features high-quality seven-day forecasts and weather reports for over two million locations worldwide. Highlights include global satellite plus radar for the USA, UK and much of Europe. Images can be animated with interactive elements bringing the weather to life! With our fantastic Live Wallpaper and new and improved widgets, you can instantly see the weather at your selected location before you even open the app.<br>Features include:<p>SEVEN DAY FORECASTS INCLUDING:<br>	3-hourly intervals<br>	Weather reports for over 2 million locations worldwide<br>	Temperature (Celsius/Fahrenheit) and the all important feels like<br>	Worldwide weather alerts<br>	Wind direction and speed (in your chosen format)<br>	Air pressure, precipitation amount and relative humidity<br>	Sunrise and sunset times<br>	View forecast as a graph for an alternative, easy to read outlook<br>	And morecomprehensive forecast features from Europes leading independent weather company<p>GLOBAL SATELLITE AND ANIMATED RADAR:<br>	Radar images for the USA and much of Europe<br>	Automatically shows your current location<br>	Pan and zoom functionality<br>	Tilt screen for landscape format<p>NEW! WEATHER MAPS (Available in PREMIUM):<br>	Stunning, high resolution weather maps<br>	Interactive weather icons and city temperatures<br>	Connect to MeteoEarth  switch to a 3D map view in MeteoGroups brand new app MeteoEarth at the touch of a button.<p>PLUS:<br>	Fantastic transparent widgets to suit any background colour. Varying sizes and now including a clock<br>	Live Wallpaper with current weather images<br>	Favourites settings<br>	800,000 Points of Interest<br>	Always show the weather for your current location with the My location favourite setting<br>	App2SD compatibility<br>	Interactive city search (GPS)<br>	Map of water temperatures in Europe<br>	Air pressure maps<br>	Weather Reports<br>	Weather News<br>	Tilt screen for landscape format<br>	Fast download times<br>	Available in 14 European languages<br>	No adverts<p>An in-app upgrade is also available but we will not hassle you about it and there is no obligation whatsoever to subscribe! In addition to the above features, the PREMIUM version includes:<p>	Hourly forecasts  for when timing is crucial!<br>	14 day forecasts  for planning ahead<br>	NEW! Stunning, high resolution maps with multiple layers of advanced weather information including precipitation type radar in Europe (showing the difference between rain, freezing rain, snow and so on), radar forecasts, worldwide visible and infrared satellite images, air pressure, heat maps, lightning strikes and cloud cover forecasts.<br>	Weather alerts displayed in the widgets plus the option to receive alerts in the notifications bar<br>	Ski Weather - For over 900 resorts in 17 countries including details of how many lifts are running, the number of pistes that are open, snow depth and quality and a live web cam!<br>	Beach Weather  this fantastic feature provides the UV Index and water temperatures for the Mediterranean, Caribbean and other popular holiday destinations<br>	Precipitation-type radar  Standard radar only shows precipitation but you cant tell if its rain, snow, hail etc. Change all that with this fantastic feature available on Premium.<br>	Forecast radar  Theres no need for guessing anymore  use our Premium radar feature to see the forecast.<br>	40 images for radar and satellite<br>	Wind conditions<br>	And more <p>If you do not have a Premium subscription, you can choose to show or hide the Premium features in More &gt; Settings &gt; Subscription &amp; Account.<p>Follow us on twitter.com/weatherpro for status updates or visit www.weatherpro.eu for more information about WeatherPro.<p>If you have any queries or concerns please email <a href="mailto:support@android.weatherpro.eu">support@android.weatherpro.eu</a> and we will get back to you as soon as possible.</div> <div class="show-more-end"></div> </div>  <div class="play-button show-more small"> Read more </div> <div class="play-button expand-close"> <div class="close-image"> </div> </div>  </div> <div class="details-section-divider"></div> </div> </div><div data-docid="com.mg.android" class="details-wrapper apps"> <div class="details-section highlighted-review" style="display:none"> <div class="highlighted-section-contents"> <div style="display:none" class="review-help unowned-app" data-unowned-docid="com.mg.android"> <div class="review-panel-content"> <div class="review-panel-close"></div> <div class="review-row"> You must install this app before submitting a review. </div> </div> <div class="write-review-triangle-container"></div> </div> <div style="display:none" class="review-help gplus-signup"> <div class="review-panel-content"> <div class="review-panel-close"></div> <div class="review-row"> Google Play reviews now use Google+ so it's easier to see opinions from people you care about. in the background and monitors the official National Weather Service (NWS) alerts for your area.  New alerts will appear on the status bar, and by selecting it, you can read the details.<p>You can also choose how urgent of a notification to get, based on the NWS Severity.  An Extreme alert coming through?  Then you&#39;d probably like vibrate, lights AND bell for that!  But a simple Wind Warning?  Probably not as much.  You can choose the level of response in the preferences.<p>Pro Weather Alert has all of the features of Simple Weather Alert, and more!<p>+ No ads.<br>+ Monitor unlimited locations, each with an intuitive name you set.<br>+ See the details and instructions of all alerts for all areas.<br>+ See where around you the alerts are using the Alert Map.  No more wondering if you&#39;re driving into or out of bad weather.<br>+ Choose how to be notified (lights, bell, vibrate), and decide which alerts will override your phone silence settings.<br>+ Sort and Filter the alerts in the list, by severity or location.<br>+ Two alert levels (emergency and urgent) are customizable, in case you want lights, bell, and vibrate for extreme alerts, and just lights for severe alerts.  All other weather alerts will give a simple notice on the action bar.<br>+ Individually select which NWS alerts you want to be considered &quot;Emergency&quot; or &quot;Urgent&quot;<br>+ Alerts keep updated automatically as long as you have connectivity<br>+ Find your alert location by GPS or network location, and have alerts follow your phone as you move.<br>+ An app widget added to your home screen allows for easy on/off toggling of lights, vibrate and sound settings.  The alerts will still be checked and put on your status bar though, so you can keep an eye on it during class or church, without it causing distraction.  You can also toggle the location following feature to save battery when not driving.<br>+ Key words and phrases list. Create a list of words or phrases, and when an alert is received that contains those words or phrases, it will be marked in the alerts list with an icon, and the phrases will be highlighted when you read the alert details.<br>+ Email an alert to friends or send via text message (**requires Contacts List permission**), so they can be warned as well.<br>+ Post your alert to our Facebook wall or Twitter feed!  This is especially useful for non-weather alerts, such as Child Abduction Emergencies.<br>+ Change your alert polling times to maximize battery life.<br>+ Constant alerting annoying?  You can now mute repeated alerts so those busy storm nights don&#39;t un-necessarily alert you.<p>NOTE:  Do *NOT* use RAM or memory clearing apps. The contacts list permission allows for easier selecting of the number.<p>IMPORTANT: While we take all possible precautions to make sure this app will get you critical alerts on time, the unforseen can still occur, as well as simple cell/network outages.
